<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a> (657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interés</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto iméjet <b>interés</b> dlja vas.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This is of interest to you.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сах</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>interésax</b> míra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the interest of peace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>interés</b> k</i> ― <span class="e-translation">interest in (+ dative)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">interésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interésno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-интере́сно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)интере́снее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-интере́сно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)интере́сней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interestingly, in an interesting manner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказывать.html>расска́зывает</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>interésno</b> rasskázyvajet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">His way of retelling is quite interesting.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">He retells interestingly.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">interésno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">interésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произведение.html>произведе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:довольно.html>дово́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интересно.html>интере́сно</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto proizvedénije dovólʹno <b>interésno</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This (literary) work is rather interesting.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ин<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тёр</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ци<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>на́ль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

***интернет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́т</a> (5847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Internet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intɛrnɛ́t</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>the Internet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́те</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko vy včerá sidéli v <b>intɛrnɛ́te</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How long did you hang out on the <b>internet</b> yesterday?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The plural form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интернет.html>интерне́ты</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">intɛrnɛ́ty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used in a humorous way, like internets (from G. W. Bush).
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерпретатор.html>интерпрета́тор</a> (32207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерпретатор.html>интерпрета́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intɛrpretátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерпретатор.html>интерпрета́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерпретатор.html>интерпрета́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интерпретатор.html>интерпрета́торов</a></b>)

<p><b>ин<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тёр</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пря.html>пре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тор.html>тор</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:интрига.html>интри́га</a> (8373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интрига.html>интри́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intríga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интрига.html>интри́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интрига.html>интри́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интрига.html>интри́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>intrigue, plot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also in literature</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> amour, gallantry, love affair</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">intrigant</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интриган.html>интрига́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">intrigán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интриган.html>интрига́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интриган.html>интрига́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:интриган.html>интрига́нов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">интрига́нка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> schemer, conspirator</li></ol>
